How to run this project?
1) log into voetbal.nl and retrieve the voetbalnl.session.value
2) place this value in application.properties
3) start application
4) navigate to http://localhost:8080/swagger-ui.html
5) use request below to search for clubs near Rotterdam

Request for clubs near Rotterdam:
{
  "cityname": "Rotterdam",
  "latitude": 51.9244201,
  "longitude": 4.4777325999999675,
  "radius": 25
}

result 09-10-2019:
